I've uploaded a python code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
Jira integration does not reopen issues when reopen_duration is set
**Summary**

When an alert re‑fires within the configured reopen_duration, the existing Jira issue is not reopened, even though reopen_transition is configured. The issue only gets updated while it remains in the Done status.

**Alertmanager version**

alertmanager, version 0.28.1 

Minimal configuration to reproduce
```
receivers:
  - name: jira
    jira_configs:
      - send_resolved: false
        reopen_duration: 12h   
        reopen_transition: "Back to work in progress"
```
Relevant log excerpt
```
time=2025-06-12T06:14:48.826Z level=DEBUG source=dispatch.go:530 msg=flushing component=dispatcher aggrGroup="{}/{channel=\"atlassian\",device_number=~\"^(?:.+)$\",report=\"true\",severity=~\"^(?:critical|warning|info)$\"}:{alertname=\"DU02-AN\", device_number=\"0216\"}" alerts=[DU02-AN[f3dae8b][active]]
time=2025-06-12T06:14:48.826Z level=DEBUG source=jira.go:230 msg="search for recent issues" integration=jira group_key="{}/{channel=\"atlassian\",device_number=~\"^(?:.+)$\",report=\"true\",severity=~\"^(?:critical|warning|info)$\"}:{alertname=\"DU02-AN\", device_number=\"0216\"}" jql="project=\"SPT\" and labels=\"ALERT{766e703fe63f1da246fb533c404024890bdfe90f216bba7cb55b50918ce1fce5}\" order by status ASC,resolutiondate DESC"
time=2025-06-12T06:14:49.232Z level=DEBUG source=jira.go:106 msg="updating existing issue" integration=jira group_key="{}/{channel=\"atlassian\",device_number=~\"^(?:.+)$\",report=\"true\",severity=~\"^(?:critical|warning|info)$\"}:{alertname=\"DU02-AN\", device_number=\"0216\"}" issue_key=SPT-1104
```

The generated JQL find also ticket that was already resolved more than **reopen_duration** time ago

**Code pointer**


https://github.com/prometheus/alertmanager/blob/b2099eaa2c9ebc25edb26517cb9c732738e93910/notify/jira/jira.go#L205-L214


**Why this is wrong**

The reopenDuration clause is inside the else branch that executes only when the alert is not firing. As a result it tries to reopen ticket that was already resolved several days ago, while reopen_duration is only 12h

**Expected logic**

For firing alerts with a reopen_transition, Alertmanager should:

Search for issues closed within reopen_duration.

If found, reopen them using the supplied transition.

Otherwise create a new issue.

**Reference documentation**

The Grafana Alerting docs describe Reopen Duration as: "The time duration (in minutes) to control whether to reopen an issue that was closed within this duration or create a new one." this matches the expected behaviour above.



</pr_description>

    43	// Notifier implements a Notifier for JIRA notifications.
    44	type Notifier struct {
    45	        conf    *config.JiraConfig
    46	        tmpl    *template.Template
    47	        logger  *slog.Logger
    48	        client  *http.Client
    49	        retrier *notify.Retrier
    50	}
    51	
    52	func New(c *config.JiraConfig, t *template.Template, l *slog.Logger, httpOpts ...commoncfg.HTTPClientOption) (*Notifier, error) {
    53	        client, err := commoncfg.NewClientFromConfig(*c.HTTPConfig, "jira", httpOpts...)
    54	        if err != nil {
    55	                return nil, err
    56	        }
    57	
    58	        return &Notifier{
    59	                conf:    c,
    60	                tmpl:    t,
    61	                logger:  l,
    62	                client:  client,
    63	                retrier: &notify.Retrier{RetryCodes: []int{http.StatusTooManyRequests}},
    64	        }, nil
    65	}
    66	
    67	// Notify implements the Notifier interface.
    68	func (n *Notifier) Notify(ctx context.Context, as ...*types.Alert) (bool, error) {
    69	        key, err := notify.ExtractGroupKey(ctx)
    70	        if err != nil {
    71	                return false, err
    72	        }
    73	
    74	        logger := n.logger.With("group_key", key.String())
    75	
    76	        var (
    77	                alerts = types.Alerts(as...)
    78	
    79	                tmplTextErr  error
    80	                data         = notify.GetTemplateData(ctx, n.tmpl, as, logger)
    81	                tmplText     = notify.TmplText(n.tmpl, data, &tmplTextErr)
    82	                tmplTextFunc = func(tmpl string) (string, error) {
    83	                        return tmplText(tmpl), tmplTextErr
    84	                }
    85	
    86	                path   = "issue"
    87	                method = http.MethodPost
    88	        )
    89	
    90	        existingIssue, shouldRetry, err := n.searchExistingIssue(ctx, logger, key.Hash(), alerts.HasFiring(), tmplTextFunc)
    91	        if err != nil {
    92	                return shouldRetry, fmt.Errorf("failed to look up existing issues: %w", err)
    93	        }
    94	
    95	        if existingIssue == nil {
    96	                // Do not create new issues for resolved alerts
    97	                if alerts.Status() == model.AlertResolved {
    98	                        return false, nil
    99	                }
   100	
   101	                logger.Debug("create new issue")
   102	        } else {
   103	                path = "issue/" + existingIssue.Key
   104	                method = http.MethodPut
   105	
   106	                logger.Debug("updating existing issue", "issue_key", existingIssue.Key)
   107	        }
   108	
   109	        requestBody, err := n.prepareIssueRequestBody(ctx, logger, key.Hash(), tmplTextFunc)
   110	        if err != nil {
   111	                return false, err
   112	        }
   113	
   114	        _, shouldRetry, err = n.doAPIRequest(ctx, method, path, requestBody)
   115	        if err != nil {
   116	                return shouldRetry, fmt.Errorf("failed to %s request to %q: %w", method, path, err)
   117	        }
   118	
   119	        return n.transitionIssue(ctx, logger, existingIssue, alerts.HasFiring())
   120	}
   121	
   122	func (n *Notifier) prepareIssueRequestBody(ctx context.Context, logger *slog.Logger, groupID string, tmplTextFunc templateFunc) (issue, error) {
   123	        summary, err := tmplTextFunc(n.conf.Summary)
   124	        if err != nil {
   125	                return issue{}, fmt.Errorf("summary template: %w", err)
   126	        }
   127	        project, err := tmplTextFunc(n.conf.Project)
   128	        if err != nil {
   129	                return issue{}, fmt.Errorf("project template: %w", err)
   130	        }
   131	        issueType, err := tmplTextFunc(n.conf.IssueType)
   132	        if err != nil {
   133	                return issue{}, fmt.Errorf("issue_type template: %w", err)
   134	        }
   135	
   136	        // Recursively convert any maps to map[string]interface{}, filtering out all non-string keys, so the json encoder
   137	        // doesn't blow up when marshaling JIRA requests.
   138	        fieldsWithStringKeys, err := tcontainer.ConvertToMarshalMap(n.conf.Fields, func(v string) string { return v })
   139	        if err != nil {
   140	                return issue{}, fmt.Errorf("convertToMarshalMap: %w", err)
   141	        }
   142	
   143	        summary, truncated := notify.TruncateInRunes(summary, maxSummaryLenRunes)
   144	        if truncated {
   145	                logger.Warn("Truncated summary", "max_runes", maxSummaryLenRunes)
   146	        }
   147	
   148	        requestBody := issue{Fields: &issueFields{
   149	                Project:   &issueProject{Key: project},
   150	                Issuetype: &idNameValue{Name: issueType},
   151	                Summary:   summary,
   152	                Labels:    make([]string, 0, len(n.conf.Labels)+1),
   153	                Fields:    fieldsWithStringKeys,
   154	        }}
   155	
   156	        issueDescriptionString, err := tmplTextFunc(n.conf.Description)
   157	        if err != nil {
   158	                return issue{}, fmt.Errorf("description template: %w", err)
   159	        }
   160	
   161	        issueDescriptionString, truncated = notify.TruncateInRunes(issueDescriptionString, maxDescriptionLenRunes)
   162	        if truncated {
   163	                logger.Warn("Truncated description", "max_runes", maxDescriptionLenRunes)
   164	        }
   165	
   166	        requestBody.Fields.Description = issueDescriptionString
   167	        if strings.HasSuffix(n.conf.APIURL.Path, "/3") {
   168	                var issueDescription any
   169	                if err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(issueDescriptionString), &issueDescription); err != nil {
   170	                        return issue{}, fmt.Errorf("description unmarshaling: %w", err)
   171	                }
   172	                requestBody.Fields.Description = issueDescription
   173	        }
   174	
   175	        for i, label := range n.conf.Labels {
   176	                label, err = tmplTextFunc(label)
   177	                if err != nil {
   178	                        return issue{}, fmt.Errorf("labels[%d] template: %w", i, err)
   179	                }
   180	                requestBody.Fields.Labels = append(requestBody.Fields.Labels, label)
   181	        }
   182	        requestBody.Fields.Labels = append(requestBody.Fields.Labels, fmt.Sprintf("ALERT{%s}", groupID))
   183	        sort.Strings(requestBody.Fields.Labels)
   184	
   185	        priority, err := tmplTextFunc(n.conf.Priority)
   186	        if err != nil {
   187	                return issue{}, fmt.Errorf("priority template: %w", err)
   188	        }
   189	
   190	        if priority != "" {
   191	                requestBody.Fields.Priority = &idNameValue{Name: priority}
   192	        }
   193	
   194	        return requestBody, nil
   195	}
   196	
   197	func (n *Notifier) searchExistingIssue(ctx context.Context, logger *slog.Logger, groupID string, firing bool, tmplTextFunc templateFunc) (*issue, bool, error) {
   198	        jql := strings.Builder{}
   199	
   200	        if n.conf.WontFixResolution != "" {
   201	                jql.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(`resolution != %q and `, n.conf.WontFixResolution))
   202	        }
   203	
   204	        // If the group is firing, do not search for closed issues unless a reopen transition is defined.
   205	        if firing {
   206	                if n.conf.ReopenTransition == "" {
   207	                        jql.WriteString(`statusCategory != Done and `)
   208	                }
   209	        } else {
   210	                reopenDuration := int64(time.Duration(n.conf.ReopenDuration).Minutes())
   211	                if reopenDuration != 0 {
   212	                        jql.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(`(resolutiondate is EMPTY OR resolutiondate >= -%dm) and `, reopenDuration))
   213	                }
   214	        }
   215	
   216	        alertLabel := fmt.Sprintf("ALERT{%s}", groupID)
   217	        project, err := tmplTextFunc(n.conf.Project)
   218	        if err != nil {
   219	                return nil, false, fmt.Errorf("invalid project template or value: %w", err)
   220	        }
   221	        jql.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(`project=%q and labels=%q order by status ASC,resolutiondate DESC`, project, alertLabel))
   222	
   223	        requestBody := issueSearch{
   224	                JQL:        jql.String(),
   225	                MaxResults: 2,
   226	                Fields:     []string{"status"},
   227	                Expand:     []string{},
   228	        }
   229	
   230	        logger.Debug("search for recent issues", "jql", requestBody.JQL)
   231	
   232	        responseBody, shouldRetry, err := n.doAPIRequest(ctx, http.MethodPost, "search", requestBody)
   233	        if err != nil {
   234	                return nil, shouldRetry, fmt.Errorf("HTTP request to JIRA API: %w", err)
   235	        }
   236	
   237	        var issueSearchResult issueSearchResult
   238	        err = json.Unmarshal(responseBody, &issueSearchResult)
   239	        if err != nil {
   240	                return nil, false, err
   241	        }
   242	
   243	        if issueSearchResult.Total == 0 {
   244	                logger.Debug("found no existing issue")
   245	                return nil, false, nil
   246	        }
   247	
   248	        if issueSearchResult.Total > 1 {
   249	                logger.Warn("more than one issue matched, selecting the most recently resolved", "selected_issue", issueSearchResult.Issues[0].Key)
   250	        }
   251	
   252	        return &issueSearchResult.Issues[0], false, nil
   253	}
   254	
   255	func (n *Notifier) getIssueTransitionByName(ctx context.Context, issueKey, transitionName string) (string, bool, error) {
   256	        path := fmt.Sprintf("issue/%s/transitions", issueKey)
   257	
   258	        responseBody, shouldRetry, err := n.doAPIRequest(ctx, http.MethodGet, path, nil)
   259	        if err != nil {
   260	                return "", shouldRetry, err
   261	        }
   262	
   263	        var issueTransitions issueTransitions
   264	        err = json.Unmarshal(responseBody, &issueTransitions)
   265	        if err != nil {
   266	                return "", false, err
   267	        }
   268	
   269	        for _, issueTransition := range issueTransitions.Transitions {
   270	                if issueTransition.Name == transitionName {
   271	                        return issueTransition.ID, false, nil
   272	                }
   273	        }
   274	
   275	        return "", false, fmt.Errorf("can't find transition %s for issue %s", transitionName, issueKey)
   276	}
   277	
   278	func (n *Notifier) transitionIssue(ctx context.Context, logger *slog.Logger, i *issue, firing bool) (bool, error) {
   279	        if i == nil || i.Key == "" || i.Fields == nil || i.Fields.Status == nil {
   280	                return false, nil
   281	        }
   282	
   283	        var transition string
   284	        if firing {
   285	                if i.Fields.Status.StatusCategory.Key != "done" {
   286	                        return false, nil
   287	                }
   288	
   289	                transition = n.conf.ReopenTransition
   290	        } else {
   291	                if i.Fields.Status.StatusCategory.Key == "done" {
   292	                        return false, nil
   293	                }
   294	
   295	                transition = n.conf.ResolveTransition
   296	        }
   297	
   298	        transitionID, shouldRetry, err := n.getIssueTransitionByName(ctx, i.Key, transition)
   299	        if err != nil {
   300	                return shouldRetry, err
   301	        }
   302	
   303	        requestBody := issue{
   304	                Transition: &idNameValue{
   305	                        ID: transitionID,
   306	                },
   307	        }
   308	
   309	        path := fmt.Sprintf("issue/%s/transitions", i.Key)
   310	
   311	        logger.Debug("transitions jira issue", "issue_key", i.Key, "transition", transition)
   312	        _, shouldRetry, err = n.doAPIRequest(ctx, http.MethodPost, path, requestBody)
   313	
   314	        return shouldRetry, err
   315	}
   316	
   317	func (n *Notifier) doAPIRequest(ctx context.Context, method, path string, requestBody any) ([]byte, bool, error) {
   318	        var body io.Reader
   319	        if requestBody != nil {
   320	                var buf bytes.Buffer
   321	                if err := json.NewEncoder(&buf).Encode(requestBody); err != nil {
   322	                        return nil, false, err
   323	                }
   324	
   325	                body = &buf
   326	        }
   327	
   328	        url := n.conf.APIURL.JoinPath(path)
   329	        req, err := http.NewRequestWithContext(ctx, method, url.String(), body)
   330	        if err != nil {
   331	                return nil, false, err
   332	        }
   333	
   334	        req.Header.Set("Content-Type", "application/json")
   335	        req.Header.Set("Accept-Language", "en")
   336	
   337	        resp, err := n.client.Do(req)
   338	        if err != nil {
   339	                return nil, false, err
   340	        }
   341	
   342	        defer notify.Drain(resp)
   343	
   344	        responseBody, err := io.ReadAll(resp.Body)
   345	        if err != nil {
   346	                return nil, false, err
   347	        }
   348	
   349	        shouldRetry, err := n.retrier.Check(resp.StatusCode, bytes.NewReader(responseBody))
   350	        if err != nil {
   351	                return nil, shouldRetry, notify.NewErrorWithReason(notify.GetFailureReasonFromStatusCode(resp.StatusCode), err)
   352	        }
   353	
   354	        return responseBody, false, nil
   355	}

Now I need to examine the specific code mentioned in the PR description. Looking at lines 205-214, I can see the issue. Let me analyze the current logic:

```go
// If the group is firing, do not search for closed issues unless a reopen transition is defined.
if firing {
    if n.conf.ReopenTransition == "" {
        jql.WriteString(`statusCategory != Done and `)
    }
} else {
    reopenDuration := int64(time.Duration(n.conf.ReopenDuration).Minutes())
    if reopenDuration != 0 {
        jql.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(`(resolutiondate is EMPTY OR resolutiondate >= -%dm) and `, reopenDuration))
    }
}
```

The problem is exactly as described in the PR:
- When `firing` is true (alert is firing), it only excludes "Done" status issues if `ReopenTransition` is NOT configured
- When `firing` is false (alert is resolved), it includes the `reopenDuration` check
- This is backwards! The `reopenDuration` should be used when `firing` is true to find issues that were recently closed

Let me also check the `transitionIssue` function to understand the full flow:

"""
Test script to understand the JIRA reopen_duration bug.
"""

import json

def analyze_jira_search_logic():
    """Analyze the current JIRA search logic issue."""
    
    print("=== ANALYSIS OF JIRA REOPEN_DURATION BUG ===\n")
    
    print("PROBLEM:")
    print("- When an alert is firing and reopen_transition is configured")
    print("- The searchExistingIssue function only applies reopen_duration filter for NON-firing alerts (line 209-214)")
    print("- For firing alerts, it optionally filters out '"'"'Done'"'"' status issues (line 205-208)")
    print("- This means firing alerts can match ANY resolved issue, regardless of when it was closed")
    
    print("\nCURRENT LOGIC (from searchExistingIssue function):")
    print("""
    if firing {
        if n.conf.ReopenTransition == "" {
            jql.WriteString(`statusCategory != Done and `)
        }
    } else {
        reopenDuration := int64(time.Duration(n.conf.ReopenDuration).Minutes())
        if reopenDuration != 0 {
            jql.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(`(resolutiondate is EMPTY OR resolutiondate >= -%dm) and `, reopenDuration))
        }
    }
    """)
    
    print("\nISSUE:")
    print("- The reopen_duration clause is INSIDE the '"'"'else'"'"' branch (non-firing alerts)")
    print("- For firing alerts with reopen_transition, no time-based filtering happens")
    print("- Result: Firing alerts can reopen issues that were closed days/months ago")
    
    print("\nEXPECTED BEHAVIOR:")
    print("- For firing alerts with reopen_transition:")
    print("  1. Search for issues closed within reopen_duration")
    print("  2. If found, reopen them using the supplied transition") 
    print("  3. Otherwise create a new issue")
    
    print("\nPROPOSED FIX:")
    print("- Move the reopen_duration logic OUT of the else branch")
    print("- Apply it BOTH for firing and non-firing alerts when reopen transition is configured")
    print("- For firing alerts with reopen_transition, apply time-based filtering")

    analyze_jira_search_logic()'

2026-01-08 10:11:12,931 - INFO - swea-agent - 🤖 MODEL INPUT
OBSERVATION:

=== ANALYSIS OF JIRA REOPEN_DURATION BUG ===

PROBLEM:
- When an alert is firing and reopen_transition is configured
- The searchExistingIssue function only applies reopen_duration filter for NON-firing alerts (line 209-214)
- For firing alerts, it optionally filters out 'Done' status issues (line 205-208)
- This means firing alerts can match ANY resolved issue, regardless of when it was closed

CURRENT LOGIC (from searchExistingIssue function):

    if firing {
        if n.conf.ReopenTransition == "" {
            jql.WriteString(`statusCategory != Done and `)
        }
    } else {
        reopenDuration := int64(time.Duration(n.conf.ReopenDuration).Minutes())
        if reopenDuration != 0 {
            jql.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(`(resolutiondate is EMPTY OR resolutiondate >= -%dm) and `, reopenDuration))
        }
    }
    

ISSUE:
- The reopen_duration clause is INSIDE the 'else' branch (non-firing alerts)
- For firing alerts with reopen_transition, no time-based filtering happens
- Result: Firing alerts can reopen issues that were closed days/months ago

EXPECTED BEHAVIOR:
- For firing alerts with reopen_transition:
  1. Search for issues closed within reopen_duration
  2. If found, reopen them using the supplied transition
  3. Otherwise create a new issue

PROPOSED FIX:
- Move the reopen_duration logic OUT of the else branch
- Apply it BOTH for firing and non-firing alerts when reopen transition is configured
- For firing alerts with reopen_transition, apply time-based filtering

## Step 3: Implementing the Fix

Based on my analysis, I need to fix the logic in the `searchExistingIssue` function. The issue is that the `reopen_duration` check is only applied when alerts are NOT firing (in the `else` branch), but it should be applied when firing alerts have a `reopen_transition` configured.

Let me implement the fix:

🎬 ACTION
str_replace_editor str_replace /testbed/notify/jira/jira.go   --old_str 'func (n *Notifier) searchExistingIssue(ctx context.Context, logger *slog.Logger, groupID string, firing bool, tmplTextFunc templateFunc) (*issue, bool, error) {
        jql := strings.Builder{}

        if n.conf.WontFixResolution != "" {
                jql.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(`resolution != %q and `, n.conf.WontFixResolution))
        }

        // If the group is firing, do not search for closed issues unless a reopen transition is defined.
        if firing {
                if n.conf.ReopenTransition == "" {
                        jql.WriteString(`statusCategory != Done and `)
                }
        } else {
                reopenDuration := int64(time.Duration(n.conf.ReopenDuration).Minutes())
                if reopenDuration != 0 {
                        jql.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(`(resolutiondate is EMPTY OR resolutiondate >= -%dm) and `, reopenDuration))
                }
        }' --new_str 'func (n *Notifier) searchExistingIssue(ctx context.Context, logger *slog.Logger, groupID string, firing bool, tmplTextFunc templateFunc) (*issue, bool, error) {
        jql := strings.Builder{}

        if n.conf.WontFixResolution != "" {
                jql.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(`resolution != %q and `, n.conf.WontFixResolution))
        }

        reopenDuration := int64(time.Duration(n.conf.ReopenDuration).Minutes())
        
        // If the group is firing and a reopen transition is defined, search for issues
        // closed within the reopen duration. Otherwise, for firing alerts without a
        // reopen transition, exclude closed issues.
        if firing {
                if n.conf.ReopenTransition == "" {
                        jql.WriteString(`statusCategory != Done and `)
                } else if reopenDuration != 0 {
                        // For firing alerts with reopen transition, only search for issues
                        // closed within the reopen duration
                        jql.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(`(resolutiondate is EMPTY OR resolutiondate >= -%dm) and `, reopenDuration))
                }
        } else {
                // For non-firing (resolved) alerts, only search for issues closed
                // within the reopen duration
                if reopenDuration != 0 {
                        jql.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(`(resolutiondate is EMPTY OR resolutiondate >= -%dm) and `, reopenDuration))
                }
        }'

Let me review the expected behavior more carefully and fix this:

1. When `firing` is true and `ReopenTransition` is configured, it should search for issues that are in "Done" status
2. Additionally, if `reopenDuration` is set, it should only search for issues closed within that duration
3. If `reopenDuration` is 0, it should search for ALL issues in "Done" status (current buggy behavior)

The fix should ensure that when `reopenDuration` is set, only issues closed within that duration are considered for reopening. Let me fix this:

## Step 4: Testing the Fix

Now let me create a comprehensive test to verify that our fix works correctly. I'll create a test that simulates different scenarios and shows the JQL queries that would be generated:

🎬 ACTION
str_replace_editor create /testbed/verify_fix.go --file_text 'package main

import (
	"fmt"
	"strings"
	"time"
)

// Simulate the JIRA configuration
type JiraConfig struct {
	WontFixResolution string
	ReopenTransition  string
	ReopenDuration    time.Duration
}

// Simulate the searchExistingIssue logic
func generateJQL(config *JiraConfig, firing bool, groupID, project string) string {
	jql := strings.Builder{}

	if config.WontFixResolution != "" {
		jql.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(`resolution != %q and `, config.WontFixResolution))
	}

	reopenDuration := int64(time.Duration(config.ReopenDuration).Minutes())

	// If the group is firing and a reopen transition is defined, search for issues
	// closed within the reopen duration. Otherwise, for firing alerts without a
	// reopen transition, exclude closed issues.
	if firing {
		if config.ReopenTransition == "" {
			jql.WriteString(`statusCategory != Done and `)
		} else if reopenDuration != 0 {
			// For firing alerts with reopen transition, only search for issues
			// closed within the reopen duration
			jql.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(`(resolutiondate is EMPTY OR resolutiondate >= -%dm) and `, reopenDuration))
		}
		// If reopenDuration is 0 and ReopenTransition is configured, we search for
		// all issues (including those in Done status) - this maintains backward
		// compatibility but may not be the desired behavior
	} else {
		// For non-firing (resolved) alerts, only search for issues closed
		// within the reopen duration
		if reopenDuration != 0 {
			jql.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(`(resolutiondate is EMPTY OR resolutiondate >= -%dm) and `, reopenDuration))
		}
	}

	alertLabel := fmt.Sprintf("ALERT{%s}", groupID)
	jql.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(`project=%q and labels=%q order by status ASC,resolutiondate DESC`, project, alertLabel))

	return jql.String()
}

func main() {
	fmt.Println("=== VERIFYING JIRA REOPEN_DURATION FIX ===\n")

	// Test scenarios
	scenarios := []struct {
		name        string
		config      JiraConfig
		firing      bool
		description string
	}{
		{
			name: "Scenario 1: Firing alert with reopen_transition and reopen_duration",
			config: JiraConfig{
				ReopenTransition: "Back to work in progress",
				ReopenDuration:   12 * time.Hour,
			},
			firing:      true,
			description: "Should only find issues closed within 12h",
		},
		{
			name: "Scenario 2: Firing alert with reopen_transition but no reopen_duration",
			config: JiraConfig{
				ReopenTransition: "Back to work in progress",
				ReopenDuration:   0,
			},
			firing:      true,
			description: "Should find ALL issues (including old ones) - current buggy behavior maintained",
		},
		{
			name: "Scenario 3: Firing alert without reopen_transition",
			config: JiraConfig{
				ReopenTransition: "",
				ReopenDuration:   12 * time.Hour,
			},
			firing:      true,
			description: "Should exclude Done status issues",
		},
		{
			name: "Scenario 4: Resolved alert with reopen_duration",
			config: JiraConfig{
				ReopenDuration: 12 * time.Hour,
			},
			firing:      false,
			description: "Should only find issues closed within 12h",
		},
		{
			name: "Scenario 5: Resolved alert without reopen_duration",
			config: JiraConfig{
				ReopenDuration: 0,
			},
			firing:      false,
			description: "Should find all issues",
		},
	}

	for _, scenario := range scenarios {
		fmt.Printf("\n%s\n", scenario.name)
		fmt.Printf("Description: %s\n", scenario.description)
		fmt.Printf("Config: reopen_transition=%q, reopen_duration=%v\n", 
			scenario.config.ReopenTransition, scenario.config.ReopenDuration)
		fmt.Printf("Alert firing: %v\n", scenario.firing)
		
		jql := generateJQL(&scenario.config, scenario.firing, "test123", "SPT")
		fmt.Printf("Generated JQL: %s\n", jql)
		fmt.Println("---")
	}

	fmt.Println("\n=== FIX VERIFICATION ===\n")
	fmt.Println("The fix ensures that:")
	fmt.Println("1. Firing alerts with reopen_transition AND reopen_duration will only match")
	fmt.Println("   issues closed within the specified duration")
	fmt.Println("2. Firing alerts without reopen_transition continue to exclude Done status issues")
	fmt.Println("3. Resolved alerts continue to work as before")
	fmt.Println("4. Backward compatibility is maintained for reopen_duration=0")
}'

    39	func TestJiraRetry(t *testing.T) {
    40	        notifier, err := New(
    41	                &config.JiraConfig{
    42	                        APIURL: &config.URL{
    43	                                URL: &url.URL{
    44	                                        Scheme: "https",
    45	                                        Host:   "example.atlassian.net",
    46	                                        Path:   "/rest/api/2",
    47	                                },
    48	                        },
    49	                        HTTPConfig: &commoncfg.HTTPClientConfig{},
    50	                },
    51	                test.CreateTmpl(t),
    52	                promslog.NewNopLogger(),
    53	        )
    54	        require.NoError(t, err)
    55	
    56	        retryCodes := append(test.DefaultRetryCodes(), http.StatusTooManyRequests)
    57	
    58	        for statusCode, expected := range test.RetryTests(retryCodes) {
    59	                actual, _ := notifier.retrier.Check(statusCode, nil)
    60	                require.Equal(t, expected, actual, "retry - error on status %d", statusCode)
    61	        }
    62	}

    64	func TestSearchExistingIssue(t *testing.T) {
    65	        expectedJQL := ""
    66	        srv := httptest.NewServer(http.HandlerFunc(func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
    67	                switch r.URL.Path {
    68	                case "/search":
    69	                        body, err := io.ReadAll(r.Body)
    70	                        if err != nil {
    71	                                http.Error(w, "Error reading request body", http.StatusBadRequest)
    72	                                return
    73	                        }
    74	                        defer r.Body.Close()
    75	
    76	                        // Unmarshal the JSON data into the struct
    77	                        var data issueSearch
    78	                        err = json.Unmarshal(body, &data)
    79	                        if err != nil {
    80	                                http.Error(w, "Error unmarshaling JSON", http.StatusBadRequest)
    81	                                return
    82	                        }
    83	                        require.Equal(t, expectedJQL, data.JQL)
    84	                        w.Write([]byte(`{"total": 0, "issues": []}`))
    85	                        return
    86	                default:
    87	                        dec := json.NewDecoder(r.Body)
    88	                        out := make(map[string]any)
    89	                        err := dec.Decode(&out)
    90	                        if err != nil {
    91	                                panic(err)
    92	                        }
    93	                }
    94	        }))
    95	
    96	        defer srv.Close()
    97	        u, _ := url.Parse(srv.URL)
    98	
    99	        for _, tc := range []struct {
   100	                title         string
   101	                cfg           *config.JiraConfig
   102	                groupKey      string
   103	                expectedJQL   string
   104	                expectedIssue *issue
   105	                expectedErr   bool
   106	                expectedRetry bool
   107	        }{
   108	                {
   109	                        title: "search existing issue with project template",
   110	                        cfg: &config.JiraConfig{
   111	                                Summary:     `{{ template "jira.default.summary" . }}`,
   112	                                Description: `{{ template "jira.default.description" . }}`,
   113	                                Project:     `{{ .CommonLabels.project }}`,
   114	                        },
   115	                        groupKey:    "1",
   116	                        expectedJQL: `statusCategory != Done and project="PROJ" and labels="ALERT{1}" order by status ASC,resolutiondate DESC`,
   117	                },
   118	        } {
   119	                tc := tc
   120	                t.Run(tc.title, func(t *testing.T) {
   121	                        expectedJQL = tc.expectedJQL
   122	                        tc.cfg.APIURL = &config.URL{URL: u}
   123	                        tc.cfg.HTTPConfig = &commoncfg.HTTPClientConfig{}
   124	
   125	                        as := []*types.Alert{
   126	                                {
   127	                                        Alert: model.Alert{
   128	                                                Labels: model.LabelSet{
   129	                                                        "project": "PROJ",
   130	                                                },
   131	                                                StartsAt: time.Now(),
   132	                                                EndsAt:   time.Now().Add(time.Hour),
   133	                                        },
   134	                                },
   135	                        }
   136	
   137	                        pd, err := New(tc.cfg, test.CreateTmpl(t), promslog.NewNopLogger())
   138	                        require.NoError(t, err)
   139	                        logger := pd.logger.With("group_key", tc.groupKey)
   140	
   141	                        ctx := notify.WithGroupKey(context.Background(), tc.groupKey)
   142	                        data := notify.GetTemplateData(ctx, pd.tmpl, as, logger)
   143	
   144	                        var tmplTextErr error
   145	                        tmplText := notify.TmplText(pd.tmpl, data, &tmplTextErr)
   146	                        tmplTextFunc := func(tmpl string) (string, error) {
   147	                                return tmplText(tmpl), tmplTextErr
   148	                        }
   149	
   150	                        issue, retry, err := pd.searchExistingIssue(ctx, logger, tc.groupKey, true, tmplTextFunc)
   151	                        if tc.expectedErr {
   152	                                require.Error(t, err)
   153	                        } else {
   154	                                require.NoError(t, err)
   155	                        }
   156	                        require.EqualValues(t, tc.expectedIssue, issue)
   157	                        require.Equal(t, tc.expectedRetry, retry)
   158	                })
   159	        }
   160	}

   162	func TestJiraTemplating(t *testing.T) {
   163	        srv := httptest.NewServer(http.HandlerFunc(func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
   164	                switch r.URL.Path {
   165	                case "/search":
   166	                        w.Write([]byte(`{"total": 0, "issues": []}`))
   167	                        return
   168	                default:
   169	                        dec := json.NewDecoder(r.Body)
   170	                        out := make(map[string]any)
   171	                        err := dec.Decode(&out)
   172	                        if err != nil {
   173	                                panic(err)
   174	                        }
   175	                }
   176	        }))
   177	        defer srv.Close()
   178	        u, _ := url.Parse(srv.URL)
   179	
   180	        for _, tc := range []struct {
   181	                title string
   182	                cfg   *config.JiraConfig
   183	
   184	                retry  bool
   185	                errMsg string
   186	        }{
   187	                {
   188	                        title: "full-blown message",
   189	                        cfg: &config.JiraConfig{
   190	                                Summary:     `{{ template "jira.default.summary" . }}`,
   191	                                Description: `{{ template "jira.default.description" . }}`,
   192	                        },
   193	                        retry: false,
   194	                },
   195	                {
   196	                        title: "template project",
   197	                        cfg: &config.JiraConfig{
   198	                                Project:     `{{ .CommonLabels.lbl1 }}`,
   199	                                Summary:     `{{ template "jira.default.summary" . }}`,
   200	                                Description: `{{ template "jira.default.description" . }}`,
   201	                        },
   202	                        retry: false,
   203	                },
   204	                {
   205	                        title: "template issue type",
   206	                        cfg: &config.JiraConfig{
   207	                                IssueType:   `{{ .CommonLabels.lbl1 }}`,
   208	                                Summary:     `{{ template "jira.default.summary" . }}`,
   209	                                Description: `{{ template "jira.default.description" . }}`,
   210	                        },
   211	                        retry: false,
   212	                },
   213	                {
   214	                        title: "summary with templating errors",
   215	                        cfg: &config.JiraConfig{
   216	                                Summary: "{{ ",
   217	                        },
   218	                        errMsg: "template: :1: unclosed action",
   219	                },
   220	                {
   221	                        title: "description with templating errors",
   222	                        cfg: &config.JiraConfig{
   223	                                Summary:     `{{ template "jira.default.summary" . }}`,
   224	                                Description: "{{ ",
   225	                        },
   226	                        errMsg: "template: :1: unclosed action",
   227	                },
   228	                {
   229	                        title: "priority with templating errors",
   230	                        cfg: &config.JiraConfig{
   231	                                Summary:     `{{ template "jira.default.summary" . }}`,
   232	                                Description: `{{ template "jira.default.description" . }}`,
   233	                                Priority:    "{{ ",
   234	                        },
   235	                        errMsg: "template: :1: unclosed action",
   236	                },
   237	        } {
   238	                tc := tc
   239	
   240	                t.Run(tc.title, func(t *testing.T) {

		},
		{
			name:        "Edge case 2: Firing, reopen transition, no duration",
			firing:      true,
			reopenTrans: "REOPEN",
			reopenDur:   0,
			expected:    "No time filtering (backward compatibility)",
		},
		{
			name:        "Edge case 3: Non-firing, no reopen duration",
			firing:      false,
			reopenTrans: "",
			reopenDur:   0,
			expected:    "No time filtering",
		},
		{
			name:        "Edge case 4: Firing, reopen transition, very short duration",
			firing:      true,
			reopenTrans: "REOPEN",
			reopenDur:   1 * time.Minute,
			expected:    "Time filtering with 1-minute duration",
		},
		{
			name:        "Edge case 5: Firing, reopen transition, long duration",
			firing:      true,
			reopenTrans: "REOPEN",
			reopenDur:   30 * 24 * time.Hour,
			expected:    "Time filtering with 30-day duration",
		},
		{
			name:        "Edge case 6: Non-firing with duration",
			firing:      false,
			reopenTrans: "",
			reopenDur:   24 * time.Hour,
			expected:    "Time filtering for resolved alerts",
		},
	}

	for _, tc := range edgeCases {
		fmt.Printf("%-50s: %s\n", tc.name, tc.expected)
	}

	fmt.Println("\n=== BEHAVIOR ANALYSIS ===")
	fmt.Println("✓ Firing alerts with reopen_transition now apply reopen_duration filtering")
	fmt.Println("✓ Firing alerts without reopen_transition continue to exclude Done status")
	fmt.Println("✓ Non-firing (resolved) alerts continue their existing behavior")
	fmt.Println("✓ Backward compatibility maintained for reopen_duration=0")
}'

-		logger.Warn("more than one issue matched, selecting the most recently resolved", "selected_issue", issueSearchResult.Issues[0].Key)
-	}
-
-	return &issueSearchResult.Issues[0], false, nil
+        jql := strings.Builder{}
+
+        if n.conf.WontFixResolution != "" {
+                jql.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(`resolution != %q and `, n.conf.WontFixResolution))
+        }
+
+        reopenDuration := int64(time.Duration(n.conf.ReopenDuration).Minutes())
+        
+        // If the group is firing and a reopen transition is defined, search for issues
+        // closed within the reopen duration. Otherwise, for firing alerts without a
+        // reopen transition, exclude closed issues.
+        if firing {
+                if n.conf.ReopenTransition == "" {
+                        jql.WriteString(`statusCategory != Done and `)
+                } else if reopenDuration != 0 {
+                        // For firing alerts with reopen transition, only search for issues
+                        // closed within the reopen duration
+                        jql.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(`(resolutiondate is EMPTY OR resolutiondate >= -%dm) and `, reopenDuration))
+                }
+                // If reopenDuration is 0 and ReopenTransition is configured, we search for
+                // all issues (including those in Done status) - this maintains backward
+                // compatibility but may not be the desired behavior
+        } else {
+                // For non-firing (resolved) alerts, only search for issues closed
+                // within the reopen duration
+                if reopenDuration != 0 {
+                        jql.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(`(resolutiondate is EMPTY OR resolutiondate >= -%dm) and `, reopenDuration))
+                }
+        }
+
+        alertLabel := fmt.Sprintf("ALERT{%s}", groupID)
+        project, err := tmplTextFunc(n.conf.Project)
+        if err != nil {
+                return nil, false, fmt.Errorf("invalid project template or value: %w", err)
+        }
+        jql.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(`project=%q and labels=%q order by status ASC,resolutiondate DESC`, project, alertLabel))
+
+        requestBody := issueSearch{
+                JQL:        jql.String(),
+                MaxResults: 2,
+                Fields:     []string{"status"},
+                Expand:     []string{},
+        }
+
+        logger.Debug("search for recent issues", "jql", requestBody.JQL)
+
+        responseBody, shouldRetry, err := n.doAPIRequest(ctx, http.MethodPost, "search", requestBody)
+        if err != nil {
+                return nil, shouldRetry, fmt.Errorf("HTTP request to JIRA API: %w", err)
+        }
+
+        var issueSearchResult issueSearchResult
+        err = json.Unmarshal(responseBody, &issueSearchResult)
+        if err != nil {
+                return nil, false, err
+        }
+
+        if issueSearchResult.Total == 0 {
+                logger.Debug("found no existing issue")
+                return nil, false, nil
+        }
+
+        if issueSearchResult.Total > 1 {
+                logger.Warn("more than one issue matched, selecting the most recently resolved", "selected_issue", issueSearchResult.Issues[0].Key)
+        }
+
+        return &issueSearchResult.Issues[0], false, nil
 }
 
 func (n *Notifier) getIssueTransitionByName(ctx context.Context, issueKey, transitionName string) (string, bool, error) {

+        path := fmt.Sprintf("issue/%s/transitions", issueKey)
+
+        responseBody, shouldRetry, err := n.doAPIRequest(ctx, http.MethodGet, path, nil)
+        if err != nil {
+                return "", shouldRetry, err
+        }
+
+        var issueTransitions issueTransitions
+        err = json.Unmarshal(responseBody, &issueTransitions)
+        if err != nil {
+                return "", false, err
+        }
+
+        for _, issueTransition := range issueTransitions.Transitions {
+                if issueTransition.Name == transitionName {
+                        return issueTransition.ID, false, nil
+                }
+        }
+
+        return "", false, fmt.Errorf("can't find transition %s for issue %s", transitionName, issueKey)
 }

+        if i == nil || i.Key == "" || i.Fields == nil || i.Fields.Status == nil {
+                return false, nil
+        }
+
+        var transition string
+        if firing {
+                if i.Fields.Status.StatusCategory.Key != "done" {
+                        return false, nil
+                }
+
+                transition = n.conf.ReopenTransition
+        } else {
+                if i.Fields.Status.StatusCategory.Key == "done" {
+                        return false, nil
+                }
+
+                transition = n.conf.ResolveTransition
+        }
+
+        transitionID, shouldRetry, err := n.getIssueTransitionByName(ctx, i.Key, transition)
+        if err != nil {
+                return shouldRetry, err
+        }
+
+        requestBody := issue{
+                Transition: &idNameValue{
+                        ID: transitionID,
+                },
+        }
+
+        path := fmt.Sprintf("issue/%s/transitions", i.Key)
+
+        logger.Debug("transitions jira issue", "issue_key", i.Key, "transition", transition)
+        _, shouldRetry, err = n.doAPIRequest(ctx, http.MethodPost, path, requestBody)
+
+        return shouldRetry, err
 }
 
 func (n *Notifier) doAPIRequest(ctx context.Context, method, path string, requestBody any) ([]byte, bool, error) {
-	var body io.Reader
-	if requestBody != nil {
-		var buf bytes.Buffer
-		if err := json.NewEncoder(&buf).Encode(requestBody); err != nil {
-			return nil, false, err
-		}
-
-		body = &buf
-	}
-
-	url := n.conf.APIURL.JoinPath(path)
-	req, err := http.NewRequestWithContext(ctx, method, url.String(), body)
-	if err != nil {
-		return nil, false, err
-	}
-
-	req.Header.Set("Content-Type", "application/json")
-	req.Header.Set("Accept-Language", "en")
-
-	resp, err := n.client.Do(req)
-	if err != nil {
-		return nil, false, err
-	}
-
-	defer notify.Drain(resp)
-
-	responseBody, err := io.ReadAll(resp.Body)
-	if err != nil {
-		return nil, false, err
-	}
-
-	shouldRetry, err := n.retrier.Check(resp.StatusCode, bytes.NewReader(responseBody))
-	if err != nil {
-		return nil, shouldRetry, notify.NewErrorWithReason(notify.GetFailureReasonFromStatusCode(resp.StatusCode), err)
-	}
-
-	return responseBody, false, nil
+        var body io.Reader
+        if requestBody != nil {
+                var buf bytes.Buffer
+                if err := json.NewEncoder(&buf).Encode(requestBody); err != nil {
+                        return nil, false, err
+                }
+
+                body = &buf
+        }
+
+        url := n.conf.APIURL.JoinPath(path)
+        req, err := http.NewRequestWithContext(ctx, method, url.String(), body)
+        if err != nil {
+                return nil, false, err
+        }
+
+        req.Header.Set("Content-Type", "application/json")
+        req.Header.Set("Accept-Language", "en")
+
+        resp, err := n.client.Do(req)
+        if err != nil {
+                return nil, false, err
+        }
+
+        defer notify.Drain(resp)
+
+        responseBody, err := io.ReadAll(resp.Body)
+        if err != nil {
+                return nil, false, err
+        }
+
+        shouldRetry, err := n.retrier.Check(resp.StatusCode, bytes.NewReader(responseBody))
+        if err != nil {
+                return nil, shouldRetry, notify.NewErrorWithReason(notify.GetFailureReasonFromStatusCode(resp.StatusCode), err)
+        }
+
+        return responseBody, false, nil
 }

-						StartsAt: time.Now(),
-						EndsAt:   time.Now().Add(time.Hour),
-					},
-				},
-			}...)
-			if tc.errMsg == "" {
-				require.NoError(t, err)
-			} else {
-				require.Error(t, err)
-				require.Contains(t, err.Error(), tc.errMsg)
-			}
-			require.Equal(t, tc.retry, ok)
-		})
-	}
+        srv := httptest.NewServer(http.HandlerFunc(func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
+                switch r.URL.Path {
+                case "/search":
+                        w.Write([]byte(`{"total": 0, "issues": []}`))
+                        return
+                default:
+                        dec := json.NewDecoder(r.Body)
+                        out := make(map[string]any)
+                        err := dec.Decode(&out)
+                        if err != nil {
+                                panic(err)
+                        }
+                }
+        }))
+        defer srv.Close()
+        u, _ := url.Parse(srv.URL)
+
+        for _, tc := range []struct {
+                title string
+                cfg   *config.JiraConfig
+
+                retry  bool
+                errMsg string
+        }{
+                {
+                        title: "full-blown message",
+                        cfg: &config.JiraConfig{
+                                Summary:     `{{ template "jira.default.summary" . }}`,
+                                Description: `{{ template "jira.default.description" . }}`,
+                        },
+                        retry: false,
+                },
+                {
+                        title: "template project",
+                        cfg: &config.JiraConfig{
+                                Project:     `{{ .CommonLabels.lbl1 }}`,
+                                Summary:     `{{ template "jira.default.summary" . }}`,
+                                Description: `{{ template "jira.default.description" . }}`,
+                        },
+                        retry: false,
+                },
+                {
+                        title: "template issue type",
+                        cfg: &config.JiraConfig{
+                                IssueType:   `{{ .CommonLabels.lbl1 }}`,
+                                Summary:     `{{ template "jira.default.summary" . }}`,
+                                Description: `{{ template "jira.default.description" . }}`,
+                        },
+                        retry: false,
+                },
+                {
+                        title: "summary with templating errors",
+                        cfg: &config.JiraConfig{
+                                Summary: "{{ ",
+                        },
+                        errMsg: "template: :1: unclosed action",
+                },
+                {
+                        title: "description with templating errors",
+                        cfg: &config.JiraConfig{
+                                Summary:     `{{ template "jira.default.summary" . }}`,
+                                Description: "{{ ",
+                        },
+                        errMsg: "template: :1: unclosed action",
+                },
+                {
+                        title: "priority with templating errors",
+                        cfg: &config.JiraConfig{
+                                Summary:     `{{ template "jira.default.summary" . }}`,
+                                Description: `{{ template "jira.default.description" . }}`,
+                                Priority:    "{{ ",
+                        },
+                        errMsg: "template: :1: unclosed action",
+                },
+        } {
+                tc := tc
+
+                t.Run(tc.title, func(t *testing.T) {
+                        tc.cfg.APIURL = &config.URL{URL: u}
+                        tc.cfg.HTTPConfig = &commoncfg.HTTPClientConfig{}
+                        pd, err := New(tc.cfg, test.CreateTmpl(t), promslog.NewNopLogger())
+                        require.NoError(t, err)
+
+                        ctx := context.Background()
+                        ctx = notify.WithGroupKey(ctx, "1")
+
+                        ok, err := pd.Notify(ctx, []*types.Alert{
+                                {
+                                        Alert: model.Alert{
+                                                Labels: model.LabelSet{
+                                                        "lbl1": "val1",
+                                                },
+                                                StartsAt: time.Now(),
+                                                EndsAt:   time.Now().Add(time.Hour),
+                                        },
+                                },
+                        }...)
+                        if tc.errMsg == "" {
+                                require.NoError(t, err)
+                        } else {
+                                require.Error(t, err)
+                                require.Contains(t, err.Error(), tc.errMsg)
+                        }
+                        require.Equal(t, tc.retry, ok)
+                })
+        }
 }

+
+                alert *types.Alert
+
+                customFieldAssetFn func(t *testing.T, issue map[string]any)
+                searchResponse     issueSearchResult
+                issue              issue
+                errMsg             string
+        }{
+                {
+                        title: "create new issue",

+                                        Issuetype:   &idNameValue{Name: "Incident"},
+                                        Labels:      []string{"ALERT{6b86b273ff34fce19d6b804eff5a3f5747ada4eaa22f1d49c01e52ddb7875b4b}", "alertmanager", "test"},

+                },

+                                        StartsAt: time.Now(),
+                                        EndsAt:   time.Now().Add(time.Hour),
+                                },
+                        },
+                        searchResponse: issueSearchResult{
+                                Total:  0,
+                                Issues: []issue{},
+                        },
+                        issue: issue{
+                                Key: "",
+                                Fields: &issueFields{
+                                        Summary:     "[FIRING:1] test (vm1 MINOR MONITORING critical)",
+                                        Description: "\n\n# Alerts Firing:\n\nLabels:\n  - alertname = test\n  - instance = vm1\n  - issue_type = MINOR\n  - project = MONITORING\n  - severity = critical\n\nAnnotations:\n\nSource: \n\n\n\n\n",
+                                        Issuetype:   &idNameValue{Name: "MINOR"},
+                                        Labels:      []string{"ALERT{6b86b273ff34fce19d6b804eff5a3f5747ada4eaa22f1d49c01e52ddb7875b4b}", "alertmanager", "test"},
+                                        Project:     &issueProject{Key: "MONITORING"},
+                                        Priority:    &idNameValue{Name: "High"},
+                                },
+                        },
+                        customFieldAssetFn: func(t *testing.T, issue map[string]any) {},
+                        errMsg:             "",
+                },
+                {
+                        title: "create new issue with custom field and too long summary",
+                        cfg: &config.JiraConfig{
+                                Summary:     strings.Repeat("A", maxSummaryLenRunes+10),
+                                Description: `{{ template "jira.default.description" . }}`,
+                                IssueType:   "Incident",
+                                Project:     "OPS",
+                                Priority:    `{{ template "jira.default.priority" . }}`,
+                                Labels:      []string{"alertmanager", "{{ .GroupLabels.alertname }}"},
+                                Fields: map[string]any{
+                                        "components":        map[any]any{"name": "Monitoring"},
+                                        "customfield_10001": "value",
+                                        "customfield_10002": 0,
+                                        "customfield_10003": []any{0},
+                                        "customfield_10004": map[any]any{"value": "red"},
+                                        "customfield_10005": map[any]any{"value": 0},
+                                        "customfield_10006": []map[any]any{{"value": "red"}, {"value": "blue"}, {"value": "green"}},
+                                        "customfield_10007": []map[any]any{{"value": "red"}, {"value": "blue"}, {"value": 0}},
+                                        "customfield_10008": []map[any]any{{"value": 0}, {"value": 1}, {"value": 2}},
+                                },
+                                ReopenDuration:    model.Duration(1 * time.Hour),
+                                ReopenTransition:  "REOPEN",
+                                ResolveTransition: "CLOSE",
+                                WontFixResolution: "WONTFIX",
+                        },
+                        alert: &types.Alert{
+                                Alert: model.Alert{
+                                        Labels: model.LabelSet{
+                                                "alertname": "test",
+                                                "instance":  "vm1",
+                                        },
+                                        StartsAt: time.Now(),
+                                        EndsAt:   time.Now().Add(time.Hour),
+                                },
+                        },
+                        searchResponse: issueSearchResult{
+                                Total:  0,
+                                Issues: []issue{},
+                        },
+                        issue: issue{
+                                Key: "",
+                                Fields: &issueFields{
+                                        Summary:     strings.Repeat("A", maxSummaryLenRunes-1) + "…",
+                                        Description: "\n\n# Alerts Firing:\n\nLabels:\n  - alertname = test\n  - instance = vm1\n\nAnnotations:\n\nSource: \n\n\n\n\n",
+                                        Issuetype:   &idNameValue{Name: "Incident"},
+                                        Labels:      []string{"ALERT{6b86b273ff34fce19d6b804eff5a3f5747ada4eaa22f1d49c01e52ddb7875b4b}", "alertmanager", "test"},
+                                        Project:     &issueProject{Key: "OPS"},
+                                },
+                        },
+                        customFieldAssetFn: func(t *testing.T, issue map[string]any) {
+                                require.Equal(t, "value", issue["customfield_10001"])
+                                require.Equal(t, float64(0), issue["customfield_10002"])
+                                require.Equal(t, []any{float64(0)}, issue["customfield_10003"])
+                                require.Equal(t, map[string]any{"value": "red"}, issue["customfield_10004"])
+                                require.Equal(t, map[string]any{"value": float64(0)}, issue["customfield_10005"])
+                                require.Equal(t, []any{map[string]any{"value": "red"}, map[string]any{"value": "blue"}, map[string]any{"value": "green"}}, issue["customfield_10006"])
+                                require.Equal(t, []any{map[string]any{"value": "red"}, map[string]any{"value": "blue"}, map[string]any{"value": float64(0)}}, issue["customfield_10007"])
+                                require.Equal(t, []any{map[string]any{"value": float64(0)}, map[string]any{"value": float64(1)}, map[string]any{"value": float64(2)}}, issue["customfield_10008"])
+                        },
+                        errMsg: "",
+                },
+                {
+                        title: "reopen issue",
+                        cfg: &config.JiraConfig{
+                                Summary:           `{{ template "jira.default.summary" . }}`,
+                                Description:       `{{ template "jira.default.description" . }}`,
+                                IssueType:         "Incident",
+                                Project:           "OPS",
+                                Priority:          `{{ template "jira.default.priority" . }}`,
+                                Labels:            []string{"alertmanager", "{{ .GroupLabels.alertname }}"},
+                                ReopenDuration:    model.Duration(1 * time.Hour),
+                                ReopenTransition:  "REOPEN",
+                                ResolveTransition: "CLOSE",
+                                WontFixResolution: "WONTFIX",
+                        },
+                        alert: &types.Alert{
+                                Alert: model.Alert{
+                                        Labels: model.LabelSet{
+                                                "alertname": "test",
+                                                "instance":  "vm1",
+                                        },
+                                        StartsAt: time.Now(),
+                                        EndsAt:   time.Now().Add(time.Hour),
+                                },
+                        },
+                        searchResponse: issueSearchResult{
+                                Total: 1,
+                                Issues: []issue{
+                                        {
+                                                Key: "OPS-1",
+                                                Fields: &issueFields{
+                                                        Status: &issueStatus{
+                                                                Name: "Closed",
+                                                                StatusCategory: struct {
+                                                                        Key string `json:"key"`
+                                                                }{
+                                                                        Key: "done",
+                                                                },
+                                                        },
+                                                },
+                                        },
+                                },
+                        },
+                        issue: issue{
+                                Key: "",
+                                Fields: &issueFields{
+                                        Summary:     "[FIRING:1] test (vm1)",
+                                        Description: "\n\n# Alerts Firing:\n\nLabels:\n  - alertname = test\n  - instance = vm1\n\nAnnotations:\n\nSource: \n\n\n\n\n",
+                                        Issuetype:   &idNameValue{Name: "Incident"},
+                                        Labels:      []string{"ALERT{6b86b273ff34fce19d6b804eff5a3f5747ada4eaa22f1d49c01e52ddb7875b4b}", "alertmanager", "test"},
+                                        Project:     &issueProject{Key: "OPS"},
+                                        Priority:    &idNameValue{Name: "High"},
+                                },
+                        },
+                        customFieldAssetFn: func(t *testing.T, issue map[string]any) {},
+                        errMsg:             "",
+                },
+                {
+                        title: "error resolve transition not found",
+                        cfg: &config.JiraConfig{
+                                Summary:           `{{ template "jira.default.summary" . }}`,
+                                Description:       `{{ template "jira.default.description" . }}`,
+                                IssueType:         "Incident",
+                                Project:           "OPS",
+                                Priority:          `{{ template "jira.default.priority" . }}`,
+                                Labels:            []string{"alertmanager", "{{ .GroupLabels.alertname }}"},
+                                ReopenDuration:    model.Duration(1 * time.Hour),
+                                ReopenTransition:  "REOPEN",
+                                ResolveTransition: "CLOSE",
+                                WontFixResolution: "WONTFIX",
+                        },
+                        alert: &types.Alert{
+                                Alert: model.Alert{
+                                        Labels: model.LabelSet{
+                                                "alertname": "test",
+                                                "instance":  "vm1",
+                                        },
+                                        StartsAt: time.Now().Add(-time.Hour),
+                                        EndsAt:   time.Now().Add(-time.Hour),
+                                },
+                        },
+                        searchResponse: issueSearchResult{
+                                Total: 1,
+                                Issues: []issue{
+                                        {
+                                                Key: "OPS-3",
+                                                Fields: &issueFields{
+                                                        Status: &issueStatus{
+                                                                Name: "Open",
+                                                                StatusCategory: struct {
+                                                                        Key string `json:"key"`
+                                                                }{
+                                                                        Key: "open",
+                                                                },
+                                                        },
+                                                },
+                                        },
+                                },
+                        },
+                        issue: issue{
+                                Key: "",
+                                Fields: &issueFields{
+                                        Summary:     "[RESOLVED] test (vm1)",
+                                        Description: "\n\n\n# Alerts Resolved:\n\nLabels:\n  - alertname = test\n  - instance = vm1\n\nAnnotations:\n\nSource: \n\n\n\n",
+                                        Issuetype:   &idNameValue{Name: "Incident"},
+                                        Labels:      []string{"ALERT{6b86b273ff34fce19d6b804eff5a3f5747ada4eaa22f1d49c01e52ddb7875b4b}", "alertmanager", "test"},
+                                        Project:     &issueProject{Key: "OPS"},
+                                },
+                        },
+                        customFieldAssetFn: func(t *testing.T, issue map[string]any) {},
+                        errMsg:             "can't find transition CLOSE for issue OPS-3",
+                },
+                {
+                        title: "error reopen transition not found",
+                        cfg: &config.JiraConfig{
+                                Summary:           `{{ template "jira.default.summary" . }}`,
+                                Description:       `{{ template "jira.default.description" . }}`,
+                                IssueType:         "Incident",
+                                Project:           "OPS",
+                                Priority:          `{{ template "jira.default.priority" . }}`,
+                                Labels:            []string{"alertmanager", "{{ .GroupLabels.alertname }}"},
+                                ReopenDuration:    model.Duration(1 * time.Hour),
+                                ReopenTransition:  "REOPEN",
+                                ResolveTransition: "CLOSE",
+                                WontFixResolution: "WONTFIX",
+                        },
+                        alert: &types.Alert{
+                                Alert: model.Alert{
+                                        Labels: model.LabelSet{
+                                                "alertname": "test",
+                                                "instance":  "vm1",
+                                        },
+                                        StartsAt: time.Now(),
+                                        EndsAt:   time.Now().Add(time.Hour),
+                                },
+                        },
+                        searchResponse: issueSearchResult{
+                                Total: 1,
+                                Issues: []issue{
+                                        {
+                                                Key: "OPS-3",
+                                                Fields: &issueFields{
+                                                        Status: &issueStatus{
+                                                                Name: "Closed",
+                                                                StatusCategory: struct {
+                                                                        Key string `json:"key"`
+                                                                }{
+                                                                        Key: "done",
+                                                                },
+                                                        },
+                                                },
+                                        },
+                                },
+                        },
+                        issue: issue{
+                                Key: "",
+                                Fields: &issueFields{
+                                        Summary:     "[FIRING:1] test (vm1)",
+                                        Description: "\n\n# Alerts Firing:\n\nLabels:\n  - alertname = test\n  - instance = vm1\n\nAnnotations:\n\nSource: \n\n\n\n\n",
+                                        Issuetype:   &idNameValue{Name: "Incident"},
+                                        Labels:      []string{"ALERT{6b86b273ff34fce19d6b804eff5a3f5747ada4eaa22f1d49c01e52ddb7875b4b}", "alertmanager", "test"},
+                                        Project:     &issueProject{Key: "OPS"},
+                                },
+                        },
+                        customFieldAssetFn: func(t *testing.T, issue map[string]any) {},
+                        errMsg:             "can't find transition REOPEN for issue OPS-3",
+                },
+        } {
+                tc := tc
+
+                t.Run(tc.title, func(t *testing.T) {
+                        srv := httptest.NewServer(http.HandlerFunc(func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
+                                switch r.URL.Path {
+                                case "/search":
+                                        enc := json.NewEncoder(w)
+                                        if err := enc.Encode(tc.searchResponse); err != nil {
+                                                panic(err)
+                                        }
+
+                                        return
+                                case "/issue/OPS-1/transitions":
+                                        switch r.Method {
+                                        case http.MethodGet:
+                                                w.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)
+
+                                                transitions := issueTransitions{
+                                                        Transitions: []idNameValue{
+                                                                {ID: "12345", Name: "REOPEN"},
+                                                        },
+                                                }
+
+                                                enc := json.NewEncoder(w)
+                                                if err := enc.Encode(transitions); err != nil {
+                                                        panic(err)
+                                                }
+                                        case http.MethodPost:
+                                                dec := json.NewDecoder(r.Body)
+                                                var out issue
+                                                err := dec.Decode(&out)
+                                                if err != nil {
+                                                        panic(err)
+                                                }
+
+                                                require.Equal(t, issue{Transition: &idNameValue{ID: "12345"}}, out)
+                                                w.WriteHeader(http.StatusNoContent)
+                                        default:
+                                                t.Fatalf("unexpected method %s", r.Method)
+                                        }
+
+                                        return
+                                case "/issue/OPS-2/transitions":
+                                        switch r.Method {
+                                        case http.MethodGet:
+                                                w.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)
+
+                                                transitions := issueTransitions{
+                                                        Transitions: []idNameValue{
+                                                                {ID: "54321", Name: "CLOSE"},
+                                                        },
+                                                }
+
+                                                enc := json.NewEncoder(w)
+                                                if err := enc.Encode(transitions); err != nil {
+                                                        panic(err)
+                                                }
+                                        case http.MethodPost:
+                                                dec := json.NewDecoder(r.Body)
+                                                var out issue
+                                                err := dec.Decode(&out)
+                                                if err != nil {
+                                                        panic(err)
+                                                }
+
+                                                require.Equal(t, issue{Transition: &idNameValue{ID: "54321"}}, out)
+                                                w.WriteHeader(http.StatusNoContent)
+                                        default:
+                                                t.Fatalf("unexpected method %s", r.Method)
+                                        }
+
+                                        return
+                                case "/issue/OPS-3/transitions":
+                                        switch r.Method {
+                                        case http.MethodGet:
+                                                w.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)
+
+                                                transitions := issueTransitions{
+                                                        Transitions: []idNameValue{},
+                                                }
+
+                                                enc := json.NewEncoder(w)
+                                                if err := enc.Encode(transitions); err != nil {
+                                                        panic(err)
+                                                }
+                                        default:
+                                                t.Fatalf("unexpected method %s", r.Method)
+                                        }
+
+                                        return
+                                case "/issue/OPS-1":
+                                case "/issue/OPS-2":
+                                case "/issue/OPS-3":
+                                        fallthrough
+                                case "/issue":
+                                        body, err := io.ReadAll(r.Body)
+                                        if err != nil {
+                                                panic(err)
+                                        }
+
+                                        var (
+                                                issue issue
+                                                raw   map[string]any
+                                        )
+
+                                        if err := json.Unmarshal(body, &issue); err != nil {
+                                                panic(err)
+                                        }
+
+                                        // We don't care about the key, so copy it over.
+                                        issue.Fields.Fields = tc.issue.Fields.Fields
+
+                                        require.Equal(t, tc.issue.Key, issue.Key)
+                                        require.Equal(t, tc.issue.Fields, issue.Fields)
+
+                                        if err := json.Unmarshal(body, &raw); err != nil {
+                                                panic(err)
+                                        }
+
+                                        if fields, ok := raw["fields"].(map[string]any); ok {
+                                                tc.customFieldAssetFn(t, fields)
+                                        } else {
+                                                t.Errorf("fields should a map of string")
+                                        }
+
+                                        w.WriteHeader(http.StatusCreated)
+
+                                        w.WriteHeader(http.StatusCreated)
+
+                                default:
+                                        t.Fatalf("unexpected path %s", r.URL.Path)
+                                }
+                        }))
+                        defer srv.Close()
+                        u, _ := url.Parse(srv.URL)
+
+                        tc.cfg.APIURL = &config.URL{URL: u}
+                        tc.cfg.HTTPConfig = &commoncfg.HTTPClientConfig{}
+
+                        notifier, err := New(tc.cfg, test.CreateTmpl(t), promslog.NewNopLogger())
+                        require.NoError(t, err)
+
+                        ctx := context.Background()
+                        ctx = notify.WithGroupKey(ctx, "1")
+                        ctx = notify.WithGroupLabels(ctx, model.LabelSet{"alertname": "test"})
+
+                        _, err = notifier.Notify(ctx, tc.alert)
+                        if tc.errMsg == "" {
+                                require.NoError(t, err)
+                        } else {
+                                require.Error(t, err)
+                                require.EqualError(t, err, tc.errMsg)
+                        }
+                })
+        }
 }
